<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подправлять.html>подправля́ть</a> (29578)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подправить.html>подпра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podprávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подправлять.html>подправля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podpravljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подправить.html>подпра́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to correct</li>
<li><i>(clothes)</i> to straighten out</li>
<li>to touch up, to retouch</li>
<li><i>(beard, moustache)</i> to trim</li>
<li>to improve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подправлять.html>подправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podpravljátʹ</b> zdoróvʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to undergo treatment</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подпускать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпускать.html>подпуска́ть</a> (13348)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подпускать.html>подпуска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podpuskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подпустить.html>подпусти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to allow to approach [to come near]
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подпускать.html>подпуска́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:секретный.html>секре́тным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́лам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ix ne <b>podpuskáli</b> k sekrétnym materiálam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they were never allowed anywhere near secret materials</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to add some, to add a note <i>(of)</i></li></ol>

***подпустить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпустить.html>подпусти́ть</a> (14995)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подпустить.html>подпусти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podpustítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подпускать.html>подпуска́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to allow to approach [to come near]</li>
<li>to add some, to add a note <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подпустить.html>подпусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ирония.html>иро́нии</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:таинственность.html>таи́нственности</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>речь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podpustítʹ</b> irónii (taínstvennosti) v svojú rečʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to add a note of irony (mystery) to one's speech</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подпустить.html>подпусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шпилька.html>шпи́льку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podpustítʹ</b> špílʹku</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> to get in (have) a dig (at)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
